Overall, I am very satisfied with it. It can even be said that I found a treasure.

name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Forest Smart Room (Double bed) (Bathtub)
info:Stayed in October 2023
info:Friends
info:4 Reviews
rating:3.7
posted:Posted November 1, 2023
msg:This is not a bad review, I hope this review can give some reference to future guests.

1. Choose this hotel carefully if you are not driving by yourself, because the location is slightly remote from the scenic spot, in the innermost part of the valley and at the top of the mountain road. Taxi drivers rarely take orders because they cannot show the mileage on the meter, and it is easy to ask for the price without using the meter ( It is a common phenomenon in Jiuzhaigou scenic spots that it is best to take a taxi from a regular platform), so it is usually not possible to get a taxi from the hotel down the mountain. We just try our luck and sometimes the hotel will have a taxi to go down the mountain. (It would be better to return to the hotel from the scenic spot, but the 2022 hotel manager‚Äôs response in the Q&A that ‚Äúa free shuttle to the scenic spot‚Äù is not true!)
2. The hotel pick-up attendant has no direct relationship with the hotel. They are usually cars from the fleet. Don‚Äôt blindly trust them. Compare prices after adding your contact information. (This time we traveled from the hotel to Huanglong and back, the car provided by the hotel was better than our own. Consulted rentals are higher than 200).
3. The hotel's water restrictions are a major disadvantage. There is no warm notice on the details page. After check-in, a check-in instruction reminder will be issued: "The room is heated by a separate water storage. The weather is cold and the temperature rises slowly. The amount of hot water is insufficient for continuous use (such as using a bathtub). ) There will be no hot water in the shower room." We checked in early in the morning, and the front desk did not send check-in instructions in time. As a result, the first person took a 15-minute shower on the second night and the second person cut off the hot water in the middle of the shower (without staying in the room to use the hot water from the sink). ), wait at least two hours for the water to slowly heat up (should also depend on the weather).

To sum up, the scenery of the Earth Warehouse is undeniable, the accommodation style is also very novel, and the attitude of the guys and girls at the front desk is very good. However, compared with the refined butler-style services of Conrad, Hilton and other brand hotels, the Earth Warehouse can be said to be a fully self-service experience. I hope it can give some help to netizens who are struggling.
